import React from "react"
import { StyleSheet, ScrollView, View } from "react-native"
import { NavigationScreenProp, NavigationState } from "react-navigation"
import { useGate } from "effector-react"
import { H2 } from "@ui/atoms"
import { ScheduleTimeGroup } from "@features/profile"
import { NavigationModalHeader, Button, Field } from "@ui/organisms"
import { normalizeSize } from "@ui/normalizer"
import { colors } from "@ui/colors"
import { usePageState } from "./usePageState"
import { scheduleGate, schedule } from "./model"

type Props = {
  navigation: NavigationScreenProp<NavigationState>
}

export function CreateSchedulesScreen({ navigation }: Props) {
  const { scheduleItem, isEmptySchedule } = usePageState()

  useGate(scheduleGate)

  return (
    <ScrollView contentContainerStyle={s.contentContainerStyle}>
      <NavigationModalHeader
        onCloseModal={() => {
          navigation.goBack()
        }}
      />
      <View style={s.container}>
        <View style={s.padding}>
          <H2 title="–°–æ–∑–¥–∞–Ω–∏–µ –≥—Ä–∞—Ñ–∏–∫–∞" bold isActive style={s.title} />

          <Field
            title="–ù–∞–∑–≤–∞–Ω–∏–µ –≥—Ä–∞—Ñ–∏–∫–∞"
            textColor={colors.accent.dark}
            borderBottomColor={colors.accent.light}
            fieldStyle={s.field}
          />

          <ScheduleTimeGroup
            schedule={scheduleItem}
            onChange={schedule.event}
          />
        </View>
        <View style={[s.footer, s.padding]}>
          <Button title="–°–æ–∑–¥–∞—Ç—å –≥—Ä–∞—Ñ–∏–∫" disabled={isEmptySchedule} />
        </View>
      </View>
    </ScrollView>
  )
}

const s = StyleSheet.create({
  container: {
    flex: 1,
  },
  padding: {
    paddingHorizontal: normalizeSize(16),
  },
  title: {
    marginBottom: normalizeSize(29),
  },
  contentContainerStyle: { flexGrow: 1 },
  footer: {
    flex: 1,
    justifyContent: "flex-end",
    marginBottom: normalizeSize(42),
    paddingTop: normalizeSize(30),
  },
  field: {
    marginBottom: normalizeSize(20),
  },
})
